msg:I took advantage of the weekend to go to Nanxun Ancient Town, so I stayed in this hotel. Overall, the experience was average, with both good and bad experiences. Let me talk about the advantages first:
1. The spherical hotel is very grand, and it is very photogenic both inside and outside
2. Thank you very much to the front desk for upgrading us from the Deluxe Lake View Room to the Exclusive Lake View Room
3. The Exclusive Lake View Room has a large space, and the round bathtub is well received
Let me talk about the shortcomings:
1. The hotel is very remote, and there is not even any takeaway to order around
2. The room has a decoration smell
3. The bathroom in the room provides large bottles of shower gel/shampoo, and there is no exhaust facility (at least I didn't find a switch), so there is a little damp smell
4. The swimming pool is not open (Ctrip wrote that it would open on March 27 when I booked it before, but I found that it would open on April 2, and no one notified me)
5. There is no coffee machine, only instant coffee, and the entire mini bar is hard to describe
6. The so-called lake view is just a small puddle and a farmland, which is really not a lake view
